  <script>
   var getAccountProfile = function(callback) {
        if (document.cookie.indexOf("isAuthenticatedUser=") >= 0) {
            $.get('/account-profile').then(function (response) {
                if (typeof(response.accountId) !== 'undefined') {
                    accountProfile = response;
                }
                if (callback) {
                    callback(response);
                }
            });
        } else if (callback) {
            callback();
        }
    };
  </script>
  <script>
   var NPOlabels = {"pagina":"home","niveau1":null,"niveau2":null,"niveau3":null,"omgeving":"prod","merkId":4,"merk":"npoportal","platform":"site","omroep":null,"programma":null,"merkType":"portal","nobo":{"eventType":"home","mediaType":"general"},"omroeplabel1":null,"omroeplabel2":null,"omroeplabel3":null,"omroeplabel4":null,"omroeplabel5":null,"zoek":null,"platformVersie":"81e2b1246e3c1e1205d7e1a9fc0dced0f5bcba48"};
  </script>
  <script>
   var link = document.createElement('link');
        link.rel = 'stylesheet';
        link.href = 'https://www.npostart.nl/styles/main.81e2b1246e3c1e1205d7e1a9fc0dced0f5bcba48.css';

        parent.parentNode.insertBefore(link, parent);

  <script>
   $(function() {
        jQuery.cachedScript = function(url, options) {
            options = $.extend( options || {}, {
                dataType: "script",
                cache: true,
                url: url
            });

            return jQuery.ajax(options);
        };

        var setNPOUser = function (account) {
            var user = {
                npoId: (account.usePersonalisedServices) ? account.accountId : null,
                npoType: account.subscriptionId === 'npoplus' ? 'betaald' : 'geregistreerd',
                profielId: (account.usePersonalisedServices) ? account.profileId : null
            };
            NPO.setUser(user);
            NPO.page();
        };

        var waitForTemplates = function () {
            if (typeof placeholdersLoaded !== 'undefined' && !placeholdersLoaded) {
                document.addEventListener('placeholders_loaded', function (e) {
                    placeholdersLoaded = true;
                    waitForTemplates();
                }, false);
                return false;
            }
            var indexTemplates = function (parent) {
                var templates = $(parent).find('[data-topspin-is-templated]');
                if (templates.length === 0) {
                    return;
                }

                var supportedPlaceholders = ['{?index}'];
                var placeholderNumber = -1;
                $(templates).each(function (key, template) {
                    $(template).removeAttr('data-topspin-is-templated');
                    if (!template.hasAttribute('data-ts-panel')) {
                        return;
                    }
                    if ($(template).find('.npo-tile').length === 0) {
                        $(template).removeAttr('data-ts-panel')
                                .removeAttr('data-topspin-is-templated')
                                .removeAttr('data-ts-source');
                        return;
                    }
                    var panel = template.getAttribute('data-ts-panel');
                    supportedPlaceholders.forEach(function (placeholder) {
                        $(template).attr('data-ts-panel', panel.replace(placeholder, ++placeholderNumber))
                    });
                });
            };

            //we index switcher tiles at first
            $('.switch-input').each(function (key, switcher) {
                var components = $(switcher).data('components');
                if (typeof(components) !== 'undefined') {
                    indexTemplates('#' + components.join(', #'));
                }
            });
            //the next we index tab tiles
            if (tabs && !$.isEmptyObject(tabs)) {
                for (var tabKey in tabs) {
                    indexTemplates('#' + tabs[tabKey].join(', #'));
                }
            }

            //index others elements on the page
            indexTemplates(document);

            initialiseNPOTracking();
        };

        var initialiseNPOTracking = function() {
            jQuery.cachedScript(location.protocol + '//assets.npo-data.nl/tag/v3/npotag.js').done(function() {
                if (typeof(accountProfile) !== 'object') {
                    getAccountProfile(function(response) {
                        if (typeof(response) !== 'undefined' && typeof(response.accountId) !== 'undefined') {
                            setNPOUser(response);
                        } else {
                            NPO.setUser({
                                npoId: null,
                                profielId: null,
                                npoType: 'anoniem'
                            });
                            NPO.page();
                        }
                    });
                } else {
                    setNPOUser(accountProfile);
                }
            });
        };

                $.ajax({
            url: 'https://www.npostart.nl/topspin/cookie',
            xhrFields: {
                withCredentials: true
            }
        }).done(function(cookieValue) {
            if (cookieValue) {
                var d = new Date();
                var c = new Date(d.getFullYear() + 5, d.getMonth(), d.getDay());
                document.cookie = '_dvp=' + cookieValue  + '; expires='  + c.toUTCString() + '; path=/';
            }

            waitForTemplates();
        });
            });
  </script>
